FORM No. 155
[See rule 329]
COMPANIES ACT, 1956
Members Voluntary Winding-up
IN MATTERS OF DRAVIDIAN BOOK HOUSE LIMITED
NOTICE CONVENING FINAL MEETING
Notice is hereby given in pursuance of Section 497 that a General Meeting of the members of the above-named company
will be held at Registered office of the company situated at ‘Periyar Thidal’, New No. 84/1, (Old No. 50),
E.V.K. Sampath Road, Vepery, Chennai-600 007, on the 31st day of October, 2012 at 11.30 A.M. for the purpose of having
an account laid before them showing the manner in which the winding-up has been conducted and the property of the
company disposed of and of hearing any explanation that may be given by the liquidator and also of determining by a special
resolution of the company, the manner in which the books, accounts and documents of the company and of the liquidator
shall be disposed of.
Dated this the 24th day September 2012.
Chennai-600 007,
5th October 2012.

R. PARANJOTHI,
Liquidator.

NOTICES
NOTICE FOR ADOPTION CANCELLATION
I, S. Subramanian, son of Sri SP. S.S. Shanmugam Chettiar, Staying at No. 15, Chinna Karuppan Chettiar Lane,
Ponpudupatti, Ponnamaravathi, Pudukottai District, have taken adoption of Master Kannappan, 12 years old, Biological son
of Sri K. Adaikappan, born on 23rd July 1995, residing at No. 3/8, K.V.R. Street, Devakottai-630 302, Sivagangi District, vide
adoption deed No. 164, dated 22nd November 2007, registered with The Sub-Registrar, Ponnamaravathi, Pudukkottai
District.
As per adoption deed, Master, Kannappan’s initial and name changed as Master S. Shanmugasundaram and it is not
published in Government Gazette But, School Admission is taken at Madurai as per adopted name, ie., S. Shanmugasundaram
and the same is appearing in the School Transfer Certificate.
Now the above cited adoption is cancelled vide adoption cancellation deed No. 272/4, dated 11th November 2010
registered with the Office of Sub Registrar, Ponnamaravathi, Pudukkottai District and Master S. Shanmugasundaram shall
hence forth be known as A. Kannappan.
Salem,
5th October 2012.

S. SUBRAMANIAN.
(Adopted Father.)
